<p>The distance between two points in <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> dimensions is given by the <a href="./Geometric Distance">geometric distance</a> between them.</p>
<h1>Set of all Points</h1>
<p>The <a href="./Set">set</a> of all points in <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> dimensions over a given <a href="./Set">set</a> of numbers is indicated by placing a <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> in the exponent of the given <a href="./Set">set</a>, for example the set of all <a href="./Real Number">real</a> points in three dimensions is written as <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-msup><a href="Real Number"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-ds mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c211D TEX-A"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-TeXAtom></a><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c33"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup></mjx-math></mjx-container>.</p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Vector
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Vectors are any quantity that can not be represented by a single number. Vectors are typically represented by an arrow pointing in the direction of the vector with the length of the arrow representing the magnitude of the vector.</p>
<p>

<p>Vectors can be written using different <a href="Vector%20Notation">notations</a> and have a set of intrinsic <a href="Vector%20Properties">properties</a>, these vectors can also be transformed using different <a href="Vector%20Operations">operations</a>.</p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Scalar Multiplication
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>A <a href="Vector">vector</a> can be multiplied (sometimes also called stretched or scaled) by a <a href="Scalar">scalar</a>, this has the effect of multiplying all the components of the <a href="Vector">vector</a> by the <a href="Scalar">scalar</a>.</p>
<p>This operation can be defined using <a href="Matrix%20Notation">matrix notation</a> as follows:</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.514em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c5B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c22EF"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c5D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>where <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> is the <a href="Scalar">scalar</a> <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.514em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom></mjx-math></mjx-container> is being multiplied by.</p>
<p>Multiplying a <a href="Vector">vector</a> by <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2212"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math></mjx-container> has the effect of flipping the <a href="Vector">vector</a> around.</p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Vector Addition
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Vector addition is the process of combining two or more vectors to produce a resultant vector.</p>
<p>Vector addition can be represented geometrically in 2-d as follows:</p>

<p>Notice that vector addition is <a href="Commutative">commutative</a> as <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.514em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom space="3" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.463em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D435 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom space="4" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.463em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D435 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom space="3" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.514em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom></mjx-math></mjx-container> which is also true of <a href="Scalar">scalar</a>addition.</p>

<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Vector Subtraction
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Vector subtraction can be performed by taking the inverse of the second vector and <a href="Vector%20Addition">adding</a> it the first vector. This is defined formally as</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.514em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2212"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom space="3" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.463em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D435 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom space="4" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.514em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2212"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.463em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D435 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Vector addition can also be defined using <a href="Matrix%20Notation">matrix notation</a> as follows:</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D435 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2212"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub space="3"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub space="2"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" class="mjx-c1D44F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2026"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub space="2"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B               </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Vector Magnitude
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>The magnitude of a vector, often denoted as <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.431em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D449 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> or <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.431em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D449 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container>, represents the length or size of the vector in a given space.</p>
<p>The general equation for the magnitude of a vector with <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> dimensions is as follows</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.431em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D449 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msqrt space="4"><mjx-sqrt><mjx-surd><mjx-mo class="mjx-lop"><mjx-c class="mjx-c221A TEX-S2"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-surd><mjx-box style="padding-top: 0.394em;"><mjx-msubsup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D463 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.297em; margin-left: 0;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-spacer style="margin-top: 0.18em;"></mjx-spacer><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msubsup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msubsup space="3"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D463 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.297em; margin-left: 0;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-spacer style="margin-top: 0.18em;"></mjx-spacer><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msubsup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c22EF"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msubsup space="3"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D463 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.247em; margin-left: 0;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-spacer style="margin-top: 0.223em;"></mjx-spacer><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msubsup></mjx-box></mjx-sqrt></mjx-msqrt></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>this equation represents the <a href="Geometric%20Distance">geometric distance</a> from the origin to the point represented by the vector in a given space.</p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Dot Product
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>The dot product is an algebraic operation that takes 2 equally sized <a href="Vector">vectors</a> and returns a single <a href="Scalar">scalar</a> number. The dot product is usually denoted with a <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c22C5"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> symbol.</p>
<p>The dot product can be defined as follows:</p>

texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.463em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0; padding-top: class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B <p>Where <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> is the size of the vectors.</p>
<p>The dot product can also be defined geometrically in 2 dimensions as follows</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.514em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c22C5"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom space="3" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.463em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D435 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.514em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.463em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D435 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c63"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6F"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c73"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2061"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>where <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> is the angle between the two vectors</p>
<h1>Properties</h1>
<p>Two vectors are parallel if their dot product is 0. This is evident from the <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c63"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6F"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c73"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2061"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom space="2" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-TeXAtom></mjx-math></mjx-container> term in the 2d geometric interpretation.</p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Cross Product
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>The cross product is a geometric operation that takes 2 <a href="Vector">vectors</a> in 3 dimensional <a href="Euclidean%20Space">Euclidean space</a> and returns a <a href="Vector">vector</a> that is perpendicular to the <a href="./Plane">plane</a> between both input <a href="Vector">vectors</a>.</p>
<p>The cross product is only defined in 3 dimensional <a href="Euclidean%20Space">Euclidean space</a> and is usually represented using a <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-cD7"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> symbol. The cross product is <a href="Anticommutative">anticommutative</a> meaning <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.514em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-cD7"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom space="3" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.463em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D435 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2212"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.463em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D435 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-cD7"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom space="3" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.514em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom></mjx-math></mjx-container>.</p>
<h1>Definition</h1>
<h2>Geometric</h2>
<p>The cross product can be calculated geometrically as follows:</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.514em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-cD7"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom space="3" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.463em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D435 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.514em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.463em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D435 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c73"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c69"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6E"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2061"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mspace></mjx-mspace></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Where <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> is the angle between <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.514em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom></mjx-math></mjx-container> and <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.463em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D435 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom></mjx-math></mjx-container>. Additionally the direction of the cross product can be calculated using the <a href="Right%20Hand%20Rule">right hand rule</a>.</p>

<h1>Applications</h1>
<h2>Area of a Parallelogram</h2>
<p>To calculate the area of the parallelogram formed between <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.514em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom></mjx-math></mjx-container> and <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.463em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D435 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom></mjx-math></mjx-container> is given by the equation:</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.514em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-cD7"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom space="3" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.463em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D435 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mtext class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c41"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c72"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c65"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c61"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c20"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6F"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c66"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c20"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c50"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c61"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c72"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c61"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6C"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6C"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c65"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6C"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6F"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c67"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c72"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c61"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6D"></mjx-c></mjx-mtext></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<h1>Examples</h1>
<h2>Simple Cross Product 1</h2>

<h2>Simple Cross Product 2</h2>

<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Triple Product
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>The triple product is a combination of a <a href="Cross%20Product">cross product</a> and a <a href="Dot%20Product">dot product</a> that takes 3 <a href="Vector">vectors</a> in 3-dimensional <a href="Euclidean%20Space">Euclidean space</a> and outputs a <a href="Scalar">scalar</a>. The triple product can be used to calculate the signed volume of a parallelepiped defined by <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.514em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom></mjx-math></mjx-container>, <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.463em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D435 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom></mjx-math></mjx-container>, and <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.475em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D436 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom></mjx-math></mjx-container> in 3-dimensional <a href="Euclidean%20Space">Euclidean space</a>.</p>
<p>The triple product of the three vectors <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.514em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom space="2" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.463em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D435 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> and <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.475em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D436 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom></mjx-math></mjx-container> is defined as follows</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.514em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><a href="Dot Product"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c22C5"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></a><mjx-mrow space="3"><mjx-mo class="mjx-lop"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28 TEX-S2"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.463em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D435 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><a href="Cross Product"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-cD7"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></a><mjx-TeXAtom space="3" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.475em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D436 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-lop"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29 TEX-S2"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-mrow></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>

<h1>Examples</h1>
<h2>Intersection with Planes</h2>
<p>Find the equation of the <a href="./Plane">plane</a> that passes parallel to the <a href="./Plane">plane</a> <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c34"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2212"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c38"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2212"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math></mjx-container> which passes through the point <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2212"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c34"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c36"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2212"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c38"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container>.</p>

<h2>Intersection Vector Between Two Planes</h2>
<p>Find a <a href="./Vector">vector</a> equation with parameter <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D461 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> for the line of intersection of the planes <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c35"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math></mjx-container> and <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>

            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Lines in Three Dimensions
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>

<h1>Parametric Equations</h1>
<p>From the vector equation, we can derive the parametric equations for the line:</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 5.505em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; <h1>Symmetric Equations</h1>
<p>If all <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub></mjx-math></mjx-container>, <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub></mjx-math></mjx-container>, and <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub></mjx-math></mjx-container> are non-zero, we can express the line in symmetric form:</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mfrac><mjx-frac class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2212"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub space="3"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub></mjx-den></mjx-row></mjx-dtable></mjx-dbox></mjx-frac></mjx-mfrac></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<h1>Usages</h1>
<h2>Intersection of Two Planes</h2>
<p>The intersection of two non-parallel <a href="./Plane">planes</a> in 3D space can be found by solving their equations simultaneously, resulting in a line.</p>
<h3>Example</h3>
<p>Find the intersection of the planes given by the equations</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 5.805em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2212"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr></mjx-itable></mjx-table></mjx-mtable></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Let <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D461 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> (parameter):</p>
<p>From <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2212"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math></mjx-container>, <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container>.
Substitute into <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math></mjx-container>:</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c27F9"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mn <h2>Normal Vectors to a Line</h2>
<p>The direction vector <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.427em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom></mjx-math></mjx-container> of a line determines its orientation. Any <a href="./Vector">vector</a> <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.3em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom></mjx-math></mjx-container> normal to the line satisfies the equation <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.427em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><a href="Dot Product"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c22C5"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></a><mjx-TeXAtom space="3" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.3em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<h1>Examples</h1>
<h2>Reverse Synthesis</h2>
<p>Suppose a line is given by the system of equations</p>

<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 4.386em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D460 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c33"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D461 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2212"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c35"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr></mjx-itable></mjx-table></mjx-mtable></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>

<h2>Intersection with Planes</h2>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Visualizing 3D Surfaces
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>There are multiple methods to accurately approximate the <a href="./Surface">surfaces</a> in 3D, usually this requires flattening them onto 2D graphs.</p>
<h1>Planes</h1>
<p>A 3D <a href="./Surface">surface</a> can be partially visualized as multiple 2D graphs, where one of the variables is set to a different constant for each one. If the shape still isn't apparent a second &quot;cross section&quot; can then be taken by setting a different parameter to different constants to get a better grasp of the shape.</p>
<h2>Example</h2>
<h3><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="3"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="3"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math></mjx-container></h3>

    </div><p>Using this shape and noticing that it's an even function about <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container>, we can see that the shape forms a sphere.</p>

            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Partial Derivative
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>A partial derivative is an operation on a <a href="Multivariable%20Function">multivariable function</a> which describes the <a href="Rate%20of%20Change">rate of change</a> of the function with respect to a certain variable.</p>
<h1>Notation</h1>
<p>Partial derivatives can be written similarly to <a href="Derivative">derivatives</a> but with the <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container>'s being replaced by the <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> symbol.</p>
<p>For example the partial derivative of <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> with respect to <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> could be written as either</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mfrac><mjx-frac><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> or <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mfrac><mjx-frac><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mrow size="s"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 <h1>Definition</h1>
<p>With an <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> variable function</p>

<p>Where <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D456 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub></mjx-math></mjx-container> represents the variable with which the partial derivative is being taken with respect to</p>
<p>For example with a 3 variable function this equation would take the form when differentiating with respect to <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> (the first variable or <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub></mjx-math></mjx-container>)</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mfrac><mjx-frac <h1>Calculating</h1>
<p>Partial derivatives can be calculated the same way as normal <a href="Derivative">derivatives</a> by treating the variable the partial derivative is taken with respect to as the variable and the rest as constants.</p>
<p>For example</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 10.558em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; <p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Implicit Differentiation in Multiple Dimensions
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Implicit differentiation in multiple dimensions is a technique used to find <a href="Partial%20Derivative">partial derivatives</a> when a relationship between variables is given in an <a href="./Implicit Equation">implicit form</a> rather than solved for one variable.</p>
<h1>Process</h1>
<ol>
<li>Take the <a href="Partial%20Derivative">partial derivative</a> of both sides with respect to the desired variable</li>
<li>Use the <a href="Chain%20Rule%20in%20Multiple%20Dimensions">chain rule</a> when necessary</li>
<li>Solve for the desired <a href="./Partial Derivative">partial derivative</a> within the equation</li>
</ol>
<h2>Example</h2>
<p>Find <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mfrac><mjx-frac type="d"><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut type="d"></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mrow><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-mrow></mjx-num><mjx-dbox><mjx-dtable><mjx-line type="d"></mjx-line><mjx-row><mjx-den><mjx-dstrut type="d"></mjx-dstrut><mjx-mrow><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-mrow></mjx-den></mjx-row></mjx-dtable></mjx-dbox></mjx-frac></mjx-mfrac></mjx-mstyle></mjx-math></mjx-container> given the equation of a sphere <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="3"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="3"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="4"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup></mjx-math></mjx-container>:</p>

<h1>Generalized Equation</h1>
<p>Consider a <a href="./Implicit Equation">implicitly defined</a> <a href="./Multivariable Function">function</a> <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container>, the <a href="./Partial Derivative">partial derivative</a> of any two inputs <mjx-container class="MathJax" <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script <h2>Example</h2>
<p>Find <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mfrac><mjx-frac type="d"><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut type="d"></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mrow><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-mrow></mjx-num><mjx-dbox><mjx-dtable><mjx-line type="d"></mjx-line><mjx-row><mjx-den><mjx-dstrut type="d"></mjx-dstrut><mjx-mrow><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="3"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="3"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="4"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup></mjx-math></mjx-container> using the generalized equation:</p>

<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Gradient
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>The gradient of a function is a <a href="Vector%20Field">vector field</a> that always points in the direction of the greatest rate of increase of the function at a particular point.</p>
<h2>Definition</h2>
<p>The gradient of a function is a vector in which the elements are <a href="Partial%20Derivative">partial derivative's</a> of each of the functions parameters.</p>
<p>The gradient of an <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> variable function can be defined as</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c <h2>Example</h2>
<p>Given the function <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="4"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="3"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="3"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup></mjx-math></mjx-container> the gradient would take the form</p>

class="mjx-c5D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-mrow><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr></mjx-itable></mjx-table></mjx-mtable></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>

            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Tangent Plane
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>A tangent plane is a <a href="./Plane">plane</a> that passes through a given <a href="./Point">point</a> and has the same slope as the <a href="./Surface">surface</a> at that point. The tangent plane can be thought of as the generalization of <a href="./Tangent Line">tangent lines</a> to <a href="./Surface">surfaces</a>.</p>
<h1>Formula</h1>
<h2>Explicit Formula</h2>
<p>Given a <a href="./Surface">surface</a> defined explicitly as <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> we can define the tangent plane at the <a href="./Point">point</a> <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mo class="mjx-sop"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28 TEX-S1"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub space="2"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub space="2"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mo class="mjx-sop"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29 TEX-S1"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-TeXAtom></mjx-math></mjx-container> as follows:</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: <h2>Implicit Formula</h2>
<p>Given a <a href="./Surface">surface</a> defined implicitly as <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D439 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D450 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container>, because the function is defined as a <a href="./Level Set">level set</a>, meaning the value of <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D439 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> never changes as we &quot;walk&quot; along it's surface. The tangent plane must be plane must therefore be the direction of zero change, using this fact and the definition of the <a href="./Directional Derivative">directional derivative</a> we can determine that the <a href="./Gradient">gradient</a> of the function <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D439 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> is perpendicular to the tangent plane. Hence the tangent plane can be easily defined as follows:</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub space="2"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"
