<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Chain Rule in Multiple Dimensions
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>TO-WRITE</p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Critical Points of Multivariable Functions
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>The idea of <a href="./Critical Point">critical points</a> can be generalized to <a href="./Multivariable Function">multivariable functions</a>. For a function <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-TeXAtom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; padding-left: 0.314em; margin-bottom: -0.516em;"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" style="width: 0; margin-left: -0.25em;"><mjx-c class="mjx-c20D7 TEX-V"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-over><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-mover></mjx-TeXAtom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> of several variables, a critical point occurs where all the <a href="./Element">elements</a> of the <a href="./Gradient">gradient</a> vector are zero or undefined.</p>
<p>Critical points are important in multivariable calculus because they can indicate locations of <a href="./Local Maximum">local maxima</a>, <a href="./Local Minimum">local minima</a>, or <a href="./Saddle Point">saddle points</a> of the <a href="./Multivariable Function">function</a>. The specific nature of each <a href="./Critical Point">critical point</a> can be determined using the <a href="./Second Partial Derivative Test">second partial derivative test</a>.</p>
<h1>Example</h1>
<p>Consider the function <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="4"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="3"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup></mjx-math></mjx-container>. To find its <a href="./Critical Point">critical point</a>, we first compute the gradient:</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 7.913em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><a href="Gradient"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2207"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></a><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mrow space="4"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-stretchy-v style="height: 4.781em; vertical-align: -2.141em;" class="mjx-c5B"><mjx-beg><mjx-c></mjx-c></mjx-beg><mjx-ext><mjx-c></mjx-c></mjx-ext><mjx-end><mjx-c></mjx-c></mjx-end><mjx-mark></mjx-mark></mjx-stretchy-v></mjx-mo><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 1.578em;" justify="left"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="padding-bottom: 0.2em;"><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mfrac><mjx-frac type="d"><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut type="d"></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mrow><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-mrow></mjx-num><mjx-dbox><mjx-dtable><mjx-line type="d"></mjx-line><mjx-row><mjx-den><mjx-dstrut type="d"></mjx-dstrut><mjx-mrow><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-mrow></mjx-den></mjx-row></mjx-dtable></mjx-dbox></mjx-frac></mjx-mfrac></mjx-mstyle><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="padding-top: 0.2em;"><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mfrac><mjx-frac type="d"><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut type="d"></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mrow><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-mrow></mjx-num><mjx-dbox><mjx-dtable><mjx-line type="d"></mjx-line><mjx-row><mjx-den><mjx-dstrut type="d"></mjx-dstrut><mjx-mrow><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-mrow></mjx-den></mjx-row></mjx-dtable></mjx-dbox></mjx-frac></mjx-mfrac></mjx-mstyle><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr></mjx-itable></mjx-table></mjx-mtable><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-stretchy-v style="height: 4.781em; vertical-align: -2.141em;" class="mjx-c5D"><mjx-beg><mjx-c></mjx-c></mjx-beg><mjx-ext><mjx-c></mjx-c></mjx-ext><mjx-end><mjx-c></mjx-c></mjx-end><mjx-mark></mjx-mark></mjx-stretchy-v></mjx-mo></mjx-mrow><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0.15em; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd extra="true"></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mrow space="4"><mjx-mo class="mjx-s3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c5B TEX-S3"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 1.072em;" justify="left"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="padding-bottom: 0.2em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="padding-top: 0.2em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr></mjx-itable></mjx-table></mjx-mtable><mjx-mo class="mjx-s3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c5D TEX-S3"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-mrow><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr></mjx-itable></mjx-table></mjx-mtable></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Next, we set each component of the gradient to zero:</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 2.906em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr></mjx-itable></mjx-table></mjx-mtable></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Solving these equations, we find that the only critical point is at <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container>.</p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Saddle Point
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>A saddle point is a type of <a href="./Critical Point">critical point</a> of a <a href="./Multivariable Function">multivariable function</a> where the function does not have a <a href="./Local Minimum">local minimum</a> or a <a href="./Local Maximum">local maximum</a>, but instead has a shape resembling a saddle.</p>
<p>At a saddle point, the function curves upwards in one direction and downwards in another direction as such Saddle points can be identified using the <a href="./Second Partial Derivative Test">second partial derivative test</a>.</p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Hessian Matrix
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>The Hessian matrix is a <a href="./Square Matrix">square matrix</a> of <a href="./Higher Order Partial Derivative">second-order</a> <a href="./Partial Derivative">partial derivatives</a> of a <a href="./Multivariable Function">multivariable function</a>. The Hessian is the <a href="./Jacobian Matrix">Jacobian</a> of the <a href="./Gradient">gradient</a> of a <a href="./Multivariable Function">multivariable</a> function.</p>
<p>The Hessian is primarily used in the <a href="./Second Partial Derivative Test">second partial derivative test</a> to determine the <a href="./Curvature">curvature</a> of a <a href="./Multivariable Function">function</a> at a <a href="./Point">point</a>.</p>
<h1>Definition</h1>
<p>Given a <a href="./Multivariable Function">multivariable function</a> <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub space="2"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2026"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub space="2"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> the Hessian can be defined as</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D43B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em; <p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Second Partial Derivative Test
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>The second partial derivative test is a generalization of the <a href="./Second Derivative Test">second derivative test</a> to <a href="./Multivariable Function">multivariable functions</a> and can be used to determine if a <a href="./Critical Point">critical point</a> is a <a href="./Local Minimum">local minima</a>, <a href="./Local Maximum">local maxima</a> or <a href="./Saddle Point">saddle point</a>.</p>
<h1>Definition</h1>
<p>Consider the <a href="./Multivariable Function">multivariable function</a> <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> with a <a href="./Continuous Function">continuous</a> <a href="./Higher Order Partial Derivative">second order partial derivatives</a> in a neighbourhood around a <a href="./Critical Point">critical point</a> <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container>. The nature of the critical point can be determined by evaluating the following quantity:</p>
<p>Let <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D43B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em; margin-left: -0.057em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> be the <a href="./Hessian Matrix">Hessian matrix</a> of <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> at the point <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container>:</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-msub><a href="Hessian Matrix"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D43B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></a><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em; margin-left: 0.052em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-mrow></mjx-num><mjx-dbox><mjx-dtable><mjx-line type="d"></mjx-line><mjx-row><mjx-den><mjx-dstrut type="d"></mjx-dstrut><mjx-mrow><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.289em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup></mjx-mrow></mjx-den></mjx-row></mjx-dtable></mjx-dbox></mjx-frac></mjx-mfrac></mjx-mstyle><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="padding-left: 0.5em; <p>Then, define the quantity <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D437 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> as the <a href="./Matrix Determinant">determinant</a> of the <a href="./Hessian Matrix">Hessian matrix</a>:</p>

<p>Then because we know that for <a href="./Continuous Function">continuous functions</a>, the mixed partial derivatives are equal (i.e., <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mfrac><mjx-frac><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mrow size="s"><mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em; margin-left: 0.052em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-mrow></mjx-num><mjx-dbox><mjx-dtable><mjx-line></mjx-line><mjx-row><mjx-den><mjx-dstrut></mjx-dstrut><mjx-mrow size="s"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-mrow></mjx-den></mjx-row></mjx-dtable></mjx-dbox></mjx-frac></mjx-mfrac></mjx-math></mjx-container>), we can simplify <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D437 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> to:</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D437 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mfrac space="4"><mjx-frac type="d"><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut type="d"></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mrow><mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em; <p>The second partial derivative test states that:</p>
<ol>
<li>If <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D437 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3E"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math></mjx-container> and <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mfrac><mjx-frac><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mrow size="s"><mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em; margin-left: 0.052em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-mrow></mjx-num><mjx-dbox><mjx-dtable><mjx-line></mjx-line><mjx-row><mjx-den><mjx-dstrut></mjx-dstrut><mjx-mrow size="s"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.289em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup></mjx-mrow></mjx-den></mjx-row></mjx-dtable></mjx-dbox></mjx-frac></mjx-mfrac><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3E"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math></mjx-container>, then <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> has a <a href="./Local Minimum">local minimum</a> at <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container>.</li>
<li>If <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D437 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3E"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math></mjx-container> and <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mfrac><mjx-frac><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mrow size="s"><mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em; margin-left: 0.052em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-mrow></mjx-num><mjx-dbox><mjx-dtable><mjx-line></mjx-line><mjx-row><mjx-den><mjx-dstrut></mjx-dstrut><mjx-mrow size="s"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D715"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.289em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup></mjx-mrow></mjx-den></mjx-row></mjx-dtable></mjx-dbox></mjx-frac></mjx-mfrac><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math></mjx-container>, then <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> has a <a href="./Local Maximum">local maximum</a> at <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container>.</li>
<li>If <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D437 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math></mjx-container>, then <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> has a <a href="./Saddle Point">saddle point</a> at <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container>.</li>
<li>If <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D437 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math></mjx-container>, the test is inconclusive, and further analysis is required to determine the nature of the <a href="./Critical Point">critical point</a>.</li>
</ol>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Multiple Integral
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>A multiple integral is the generalization of the <a href="./Integral">integral</a> into higher dimensions and for <a href="./Multivariable Function">multivariable functions</a>.</p>
<p>The general multiple integral can be written as</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-munder><mjx-row><mjx-base><mjx-mrow><mjx-mo class="mjx-lop"><mjx-c class="mjx-c222B TEX-S2"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2026"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-lop" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c222B TEX-S2"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-mrow></mjx-base></mjx-row><mjx-row><mjx-under style="padding-top: 0.167em; padding-left: 1.428em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D445 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-under></mjx-row></mjx-munder><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub space="2"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2026"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub space="2"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c22EF"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>A 2d integral taken over an area <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> is written as</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-munder><mjx-row><mjx-base><mjx-mo class="mjx-lop"><mjx-c class="mjx-c222C TEX-S2"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-base></mjx-row><mjx-row><mjx-under style="padding-top: 0.167em; padding-left: 0.18em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-under></mjx-row></mjx-munder><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.167em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>and a 3d integral taken over a volume <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D449 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> is written as</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-munder><mjx-row><mjx-base><mjx-mo class="mjx-lop"><mjx-c class="mjx-c222D TEX-S2"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-base></mjx-row><mjx-row><mjx-under style="padding-top: 0.167em; padding-left: 0.427em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D449 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-under></mjx-row></mjx-munder><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.278em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.167em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.167em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D467 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Multiple integrals are solved in the same way as <a href="./Integral">integrals</a> with the most internal <a href="./Integral">integral</a> being solved first, treating all the other variables as constants and then repeating the process up.</p>

              </div>
            </div></p>
<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Polar Coordinates System
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>The polar coordinates system defines a given <a href="./Point">point</a> by using a distance and an angle as it's two coordinates instead of the standard two distances (<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> and <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container>). The two coordinates are typically <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> (the distance from the origin) and <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> (the angle from what is usually the positive <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container>-axis).</p>
<p>Polar coordinates can be extended into three dimensions using either the <a href="./Cylindrical Coordinate System">cylindrical coordinate system</a> which adds another distance coordinate, or the <a href="./Spherical Coordinate System">spherical coordinate system</a> which uses two angles and a distance from the origin.</p>
<h1>Conversion Between <a href="./Cartesian Coordinates System">Cartesian Coordinates System</a> and Polar Coordinates</h1>
<p>To convert between the <a href="./Cartesian Coordinates System">cartesian coordinates system</a> and the polar coordinates system, we can use the following formulas:</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 5.664em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c22C5"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c63"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6F"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c73"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2061"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c22C5"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c73"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c69"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6E"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2061"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr></mjx-itable></mjx-table></mjx-mtable></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>and conversely,</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 6.857em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msqrt space="4"><mjx-sqrt><mjx-surd><mjx-mo class="mjx-sop"><mjx-c class="mjx-c221A TEX-S1"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-surd><mjx-box style="padding-top: 0.173em;"><mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.289em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="3"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.289em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup></mjx-box></mjx-sqrt></mjx-msqrt><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="4"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c74"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c61"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6E"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.413em;"><mjx-TeXAtom size="s" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2212"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-TeXAtom></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2061"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mrow space="2"><mjx-mo class="mjx-lop"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28 TEX-S2"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mfrac><mjx-frac type="d"><mjx-num><mjx-nstrut type="d"></mjx-nstrut><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-num><mjx-dbox><mjx-dtable><mjx-line type="d"></mjx-line><mjx-row><mjx-den><mjx-dstrut type="d"></mjx-dstrut><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-den></mjx-row></mjx-dtable></mjx-dbox></mjx-frac></mjx-mfrac><mjx-mo class="mjx-lop"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29 TEX-S2"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-mrow><mjx-mtext class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-cA0"></mjx-c></mjx-mtext><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr></mjx-itable></mjx-table></mjx-mtable></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>

<p>
            <div class="embed">
              <div class="embed-page">
                Evaluating Double Integrals in Polar Coordinates
              </div>
              <div class="embed-content">
                <p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>Evaluating double integrals in <a href="./Polar Coordinates System">polar coordinates</a> is useful when the region of integration is more naturally described in <a href="./Polar Coordinates System">polar form</a>, such as circles, sectors, or regions with radial symmetry.</p>
<p>This method transforms the <a href="./Multiple Integral">integral</a> from <a href="./Cartesian Coordinates System">Cartesian coordinates</a> <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> to <a href="./Polar Coordinates System">polar coordinates</a> <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container>.</p>
<h1>Transformation</h1>
<p>The relationship between Cartesian and polar coordinates is given by:</p>
<p><mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;" display="true"><mjx-math display="true" style="margin-left: 0; margin-right: 0;" class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mtable style="min-width: 4.497em;"><mjx-table><mjx-itable><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-bottom: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c63"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6F"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c73"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2061"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr><mjx-mtr><mjx-mtd style="text-align: right; padding-right: 0; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd><mjx-mtd style="text-align: left; padding-left: 0; padding-top: 0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c73"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c69"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6E"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2061"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-tstrut></mjx-tstrut></mjx-mtd></mjx-mtr></mjx-itable></mjx-table></mjx-mtable></mjx-math></mjx-container></p>
<p>where <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2265"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math></mjx-container> and <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2208"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c5B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D70B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container>.</p>
<p>The area element <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> in polar coordinates is <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.167em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.167em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container>. The additional factor of <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> arrises from the <a href="./Jacobian Matrix">Jacobian</a> of the transformation from Cartesian to polar coordinates.</p>
<h1>Double Integral Formula</h1>
<p>To evaluate <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mstyle><mjx-munder><mjx-row><mjx-base><mjx-mo class="mjx-lop"><mjx-c class="mjx-c222C TEX-S2"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-base></mjx-row><mjx-row><mjx-under style="padding-top: 0.167em; padding-left: 0.152em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D437 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-under></mjx-row></mjx-munder><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.167em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-mstyle></mjx-math></mjx-container> over a region <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D437 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> in polar coordinates:</p>
<ol>
<li>Express <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D453 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math></mjx-container> in terms of <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> and <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container>.</li>
<li>Determine the limits for <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> and <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> that describe <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D437 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container>.</li>
<li>Use the formula:</li>
</ol>

<h1>Example</h1>
<p>Evaluate <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mstyle><mjx-munder><mjx-row><mjx-base><mjx-mo class="mjx-lop"><mjx-c class="mjx-c222C TEX-S2"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-base></mjx-row><mjx-row><mjx-under style="padding-top: 0.167em; padding-left: 0.152em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D437 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-under></mjx-row></mjx-munder><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.413em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="3"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D466 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.413em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mstyle><mjx-mspace style="width: 0.167em;"></mjx-mspace></mjx-mstyle><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D451 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D434 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-mstyle></mjx-math></mjx-container> where <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D437 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> is the disk of radius 1 centred at the origin.</p>
<p>In polar coordinates, <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="4"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup></mjx-math></mjx-container>, and <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D437 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math></mjx-container> is <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2264"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2264"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math></mjx-container>, <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="CHTML" style="font-size: 121%;"><mjx-math class=" MJX-TEX"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c30"></mjx-c></mjx-mn><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c
